NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

SOUTHERN LPG LIMITED

Extracts from the Minutes of the Extraordinary General meeting of the Company held
on 30-4-2015, at 10.30 AM at the Registered Office of the Company.
RESOLVED FURTHER THAT Mr. S. Babu, Chartered Accountant, Liquidator of the Company be and is hereby authorized
and empowered to exercise all powers as provided in section 457 of the Companies Act, 1956 and further authorized to file
all the necessary forms, papers, returns, documents, etc., as may be required, with the Registrar of Companies, Tamil Nanu
and / or such other authorities and / or agency(ies) as may be required, publish, issue any notices, forms advertisements,
declarations etc., and to do all such other acts, deeds, matters and things as may be necessary to give effect the forgoing
resolution.
Chennai,
for Southern LPG Limited,
8th May 2015.
SYED YOUSUF SHAH.
Director.
SOUTHERN LPG LIMITED
No. 2 (Old No. 33), Venugopal Avenue Chetpet, Chennai-600 031.
CIN U23203TN1994PLC026960
Pursuant to section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, notice is hereby given that at an Extraordinary General Meeting
of the Company held on 30th April 2015, the following Special Resolution was passed unanimously to voluntarily wind up
M/s. Southern LPG Limited.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 30th March, 2015, made by the Board of Directors
of the Company under section 488 of the Campanies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay its debts
in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company, having its Registered Office
at No. 2, (Old  No. 33), Venugopal Avenue, Chetpet, Chennai-600 031, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to section
484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
FURTHER RESOLVED THAT Mr. S. Babu, Chartered Accountant, residing at C3, A Block, Ganesha Flats, No. 267,
Velachery Main Road, Velachery, Chennai-600 042, be and is hereby appointed as Liquidator of the Company for the
purpose of winding up on a remuneration of Rs.50,000/- plus out of pocket expenses as actual.
Chennai,
SYED YOUSUF SHAH,
8th May 2015.
Director.
